<p><strong>Features</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Allows interaction with the main content</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports dragging and resizing</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports minimizing and maximizing the panel</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Controlled and uncontrolled size and position</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports snapping to a grid</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports locking the aspect ratio</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports closing on escape key</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports persisting size and position when closed</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="anatomy" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Anatomy<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#anatomy"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Check the floating panel anatomy and part names.</p>

<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute to help identify them in the DOM.</p>

<p>Import the floating panel package:</p>

<h3 id="resizing" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Resizing<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#resizing"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<h4 id="setting-the-initial-size" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Setting the initial size<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-initial-size"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<p>To set the initial size of the floating panel, you can pass the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultSize</code>
prop to the machine.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>floatingPanel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  defaultSize<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> width<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">300</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> height<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">300</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h4 id="controlling-the-size" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Controlling the size<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlling-the-size"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">size</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onSizeChange</code> to control size externally.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>floatingPanel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  size<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> width<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">300</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> height<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">300</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onSizeChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { size: { width: number, height: number } }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;floating panel is:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">size</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">width</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">size</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">height</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h4 id="disable-resizing" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Disable resizing<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disable-resizing"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<p>By default, the panel can be resized by dragging its edges (resize handles). To
disable this behavior, set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">resizable</code> prop to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">false</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>floatingPanel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  resizable<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h4 id="setting-size-constraints" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Setting size constraints<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-size-constraints"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<p>You can also control the minimum allowed dimensions of the panel by using the
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">minSize</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">maxSize</code> props.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>floatingPanel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  minSize<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> width<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">100</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> height<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">100</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  maxSize<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> width<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">500</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> height<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">500</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="aspect-ratio" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Aspect ratio<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#aspect-ratio"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To lock the aspect ratio of the floating panel, set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">lockAspectRatio</code> prop.
This will ensure the panel maintains a consistent aspect ratio while being
resized.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>floatingPanel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  lockAspectRatio<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="positioning" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Positioning<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#positioning"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<h4 id="setting-the-initial-position" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Setting the initial position<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-initial-position"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<p>To specify the initial position of the floating panel, use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultPosition</code>
prop. If <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultPosition</code> is not provided, the floating panel will be initially
positioned at the center of the viewport.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>floatingPanel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  defaultPosition<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> x<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">500</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> y<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">200</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h4 id="anchor-position" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Anchor position<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#anchor-position"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<p>An alternative to setting the initial position is to provide a function that
returns the anchor position. This function is called when the panel is opened
and receives the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">triggerRect</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">boundaryRect</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>floatingPanel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function">getAnchorPosition</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> triggerRect<span class="token punctuation">,</span> boundaryRect <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      x<span class="token operator">:</span> boundaryRect<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">x</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>boundaryRect<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">width</span> <span class="token operator">-</span> triggerRect<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">width</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">/</span> <span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      y<span class="token operator">:</span> boundaryRect<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">y</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>boundaryRect<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">height</span> <span class="token operator">-</span> triggerRect<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">height</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">/</span> <span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h4 id="controlling-the-position" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Controlling the position<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlling-the-position"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<p>To control the position of the floating panel programmatically, you can pass the
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">position</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onPositionChange</code> prop to the machine.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>floatingPanel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  position<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> x<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">500</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> y<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">200</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onPositionChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { position: { x: number, y: number } }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;floating panel is:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">position</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">x</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">position</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">y</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h4 id="disable-dragging" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Disable dragging<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disable-dragging"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<p>The floating panel enables you to set its position and move it by dragging. To
disable this behavior, set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">draggable</code> prop to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">false</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>floatingPanel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  draggable<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h4 id="controlling-positioning-strategy" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Controlling positioning strategy<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlling-positioning-strategy"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">strategy</code> to control positioning behavior (<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">fixed</code> or <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">absolute</code>).</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>floatingPanel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  strategy<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;absolute&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h4 id="snapping-to-a-grid" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Snapping to a grid<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#snapping-to-a-grid"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">gridSize</code> to snap drag and resize interactions to a grid.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>floatingPanel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  gridSize<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">8</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h4 id="allowing-overflow-outside-boundaries" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Allowing overflow outside boundaries<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#allowing-overflow-outside-boundaries"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">allowOverflow</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code> to let the panel move outside boundary limits.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>floatingPanel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  allowOverflow<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="events" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Events<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#events"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The floating panel generates a variety of events that you can handle.</p>
<h4 id="open-state" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Open State<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#open-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<p>When the floating panel is <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">opened</code> or <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closed</code>, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onOpenChange</code> callback is
invoked.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>floatingPanel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function">onOpenChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { open: boolean }</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;floating panel is:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">open</span> <span class="token operator">?</span> <span class="token string">&quot;opened&quot;</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;closed&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h4 id="position-change" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Position Change<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#position-change"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<p>When the position of the floating panel changes, these callbacks are invoked:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onPositionChange</code> — When the position of the floating panel changes.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onPositionChangeEnd</code> — When the position of the floating panel changes ends.</li>
</ul>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>floatingPanel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function">onPositionChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { position: { x: number, y: number } }</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;floating panel is:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">position</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">x</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">position</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">y</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onPositionChangeEnd</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { position: { x: number, y: number } }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;floating panel is:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">position</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">x</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">position</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">y</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h4 id="resize" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Resize<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#resize"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<p>When the size of the floating panel changes, these callbacks are invoked:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onSizeChange</code> — When the panel size changes.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onSizeChangeEnd</code> — When panel resizing ends.</li>
</ul>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>floatingPanel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function">onSizeChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { size: { width: number, height: number } }</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;floating panel is:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">size</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">width</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">size</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">height</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onSizeChangeEnd</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { size: { width: number, height: number } }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;floating panel is:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">size</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">width</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">size</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">height</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h4 id="minimizing-and-maximizing" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Minimizing and Maximizing<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#minimizing-and-maximizing"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<p>The floating panel can be minimized, default, and maximized by clicking the
respective buttons in the header. We refer to this as the panel&#x27;s <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">stage</code>.</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">
<p>When the panel is minimized, the body is hidden and the panel is resized to a
minimum size.</p>
</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">
<p>When the panel is maximized, the panel scales to the match the size of the
defined boundary rect (via <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getBoundaryEl</code> prop).</p>
</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">
<p>When the panel is restored, the panel is resized back to the previously known
size.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>When the stage changes, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onStageChange</code> callback is invoked.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>floatingPanel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function">onStageChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { stage: &quot;minimized&quot; | &quot;maximized&quot; | &quot;default&quot; }</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;floating panel is:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">stage</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="persisting-size-and-position-when-closed" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Persisting size and position when closed<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#persisting-size-and-position-when-closed"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">persistRect</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code> to preserve size and position across close and
reopen.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>floatingPanel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  persistRect<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="customizing-accessibility-labels" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Customizing accessibility labels<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#customizing-accessibility-labels"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">translations</code> to customize stage control labels.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>floatingPanel<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  translations<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    minimize<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Minimize panel&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    maximize<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Maximize panel&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    restore<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Restore panel&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>The floating panel component uses data attributes to style its various parts.
Each part has a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-scope=&quot;floating-panel&quot;</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute that you
can use to target specific elements.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;floating-panel&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;content&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* Add styles for the main panel container */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;floating-panel&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;body&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* Add styles for the panel&#x27;s content area */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;floating-panel&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;header&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* Add styles for the panel&#x27;s header */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;floating-panel&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;stage-trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* Add styles for state buttons in the header */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;floating-panel&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;resize-trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* Add styles for resize handles */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">

</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;floating-panel&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;resize-trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-axis</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;s&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

<h3 id="dragging" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Dragging<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#dragging"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When dragging the panel, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">[data-dragging]</code> attribute is applied to the
panel.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;floating-panel&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;content&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-dragging</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* Add styles for dragging state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="stacking" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Stacking<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#stacking"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The floating panel has several states that can be targeted using data
attributes:</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">/* When the panel is the topmost element */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;floating-panel&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;content&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-topmost</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* Add styles for topmost state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">/* When the panel is behind another panel */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;floating-panel&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;content&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-behind</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* Add styles for behind state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The floating panel machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ trigger: string; positioner: string; content: string; title: string; header: string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the elements in the floating panel. Useful for composition.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">translations</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">IntlTranslations</code><span class="d_block">The translations for the floating panel.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">strategy</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;absolute&quot; | &quot;fixed&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The strategy to use for positioning</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">allowOverflow</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the panel should be strictly contained within the boundary when dragging</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">open</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">The controlled open state of the panel</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultOpen</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">The initial open state of the panel when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the open state of the panel.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">resizable</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the panel is resizable</span></li><li class="d_flex prose">size</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Size</code><span class="d_block">The size of the panel</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultSize</code><code class="fs_sm class="d_block">The minimum size of the panel</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em prose">defaultPosition</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Point</code><span class="d_block">The initial position of the panel when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the position of the panel.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getAnchorPosition</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: AnchorPositionDetails) =&gt; Point</code><span class="d_block">Function that returns the initial position of the panel when it is opened.

Useful for recalculating the boundary rect when
the it is resized.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disabled</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the panel is disabled</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onPositionChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: PositionChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the position of the panel changes via dragging</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onPositionChangeEnd</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: PositionChangeDetails) =&gt; <h3 id="machine-api" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine API<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-api"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The floating panel <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">open</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the panel is open</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">setOpen</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(open: boolean) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to open or close the panel</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dragging</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the panel is being dragged</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">resizing</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the panel is being resized</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">position</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Point</code><span class="d_block">The position of the panel</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">setPosition</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(position: Point) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to set the position of the panel</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">size</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Size</code><span class="d_block">The size of the panel</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">setSize</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(size: Size) =&gt; <h3 id="data-attributes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Data Attributes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#data-attributes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>

floating panel is a detachable window that floats above the main interface,\ntypically used for displaying and editing properties. The panel can be dragged,\nresized, and positioned anywhere on the screen for optimal workflow.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThink of the panel that pops up in Figma when you click \u003ccode\u003evariables\u003c/code\u003e or try to\nset a color.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cresources pkg=\"@zag-js/floating-panel\"\u003e\n\u003cshowcase id=\"FloatingPanel\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFeatures\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAllows interaction with the main content\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports dragging and resizing\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports minimizing and maximizing the panel\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eControlled and uncontrolled size and position\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports snapping to a grid\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports locking the aspect ratio\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports closing on escape key\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports persisting size and position when closed\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eInstallation\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eInstall the floating panel package:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"floating-panel/installation.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eAnatomy\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eCheck the floating panel anatomy and part names.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eEach part includes a \u003ccode\u003edata-part\u003c/code\u003e attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003canatomy id=\"floating-panel\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eUsage\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eImport the floating panel package:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003eimport * as floatingPanel from \"@zag-js/floating-panel\"\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThese are the key exports:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003emachine\u003c/code\u003e - State machine logic.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003econnect\u003c/code\u003e - Maps behavior to JSX props and event handlers.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThen use the framework integration helpers:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"floating-panel/usage.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eResizing\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eSetting the initial size\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo set the initial size of the floating panel, you can pass the \u003ccode\u003edefaultSize\u003c/code\u003e\nprop to the machine.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(floatingPanel.machine, {\n  defaultSize: { width: 300, height: 300 },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eControlling the size\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003esize\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eonSizeChange\u003c/code\u003e to control size externally.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(floatingPanel.machine, {\n  size: { width: 300, height: 300 },\n  onSizeChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { size: { width: number, height: number } }\n    console.log(\"floating panel is:\", details.size.width, details.size.height)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eDisable resizing\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eBy default, the panel can be resized by dragging its edges (resize handles). To\ndisable this behavior, set the \u003ccode\u003eresizable\u003c/code\u003e prop to \u003ccode\u003efalse\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(floatingPanel.machine, {\n  resizable: false,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eSetting size constraints\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eYou can also control the minimum allowed dimensions of the panel by using the\n\u003ccode\u003eminSize\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003emaxSize\u003c/code\u003e props.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\" metastring=\"{2,3}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(floatingPanel.machine, {\n  minSize: { width: 100, height: 100 },\n  maxSize: { width: 500, height: 500 },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eAspect ratio\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo lock the aspect ratio of the floating panel, set the \u003ccode\u003elockAspectRatio\u003c/code\u003e prop.\nThis will ensure the panel maintains a consistent aspect ratio while being\nresized.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(floatingPanel.machine, {\n  lockAspectRatio: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003ePositioning\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eSetting the initial position\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo specify the initial position of the floating panel, use the \u003ccode\u003edefaultPosition\u003c/code\u003e\nprop. If \u003ccode\u003edefaultPosition\u003c/code\u003e is not provided, the floating panel will be initially\npositioned at the center of the viewport.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(floatingPanel.machine, {\n  defaultPosition: { x: 500, y: 200 },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eAnchor position\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eAn alternative to setting the initial position is to provide a function that\nreturns the anchor position. This function is called when the panel is opened\nand receives the \u003ccode\u003etriggerRect\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eboundaryRect\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(floatingPanel.machine, {\n  getAnchorPosition({ triggerRect, boundaryRect }) {\n    return {\n      x: boundaryRect.x + (boundaryRect.width - triggerRect.width) / 2,\n      y: boundaryRect.y + (boundaryRect.height - triggerRect.height) / 2,\n    }\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eControlling the position\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo control the position of the floating panel programmatically, you can pass the\n\u003ccode\u003eposition\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eonPositionChange\u003c/code\u003e prop to the machine.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(floatingPanel.machine, {\n  position: { x: 500, y: 200 },\n  onPositionChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { position: { x: number, y: number } }\n    console.log(\"floating panel is:\", details.position.x, details.position.y)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eDisable dragging\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe floating panel enables you to set its position and move it by dragging. To\ndisable this behavior, set the \u003ccode\u003edraggable\u003c/code\u003e prop to \u003ccode\u003efalse\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(floatingPanel.machine, {\n  draggable: false,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eControlling positioning strategy\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003estrategy\u003c/code\u003e to control positioning behavior (\u003ccode\u003efixed\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003eabsolute\u003c/code\u003e).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(floatingPanel.machine, {\n  strategy: \"absolute\",\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eSnapping to a grid\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003egridSize\u003c/code\u003e to snap drag and resize interactions to a grid.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(floatingPanel.machine, {\n  gridSize: 8,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eAllowing overflow outside boundaries\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSet \u003ccode\u003eallowOverflow\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003etrue\u003c/code\u003e to let the panel move outside boundary limits.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(floatingPanel.machine, {\n  allowOverflow: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eEvents\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe floating panel generates a variety of events that you can handle.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eOpen State\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen the floating panel is \u003ccode\u003eopened\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003eclosed\u003c/code\u003e, },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003ePosition Change\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen the position of the floating panel changes, these callbacks are invoked:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eonPositionChange\u003c/code\u003e — When the position of the floating panel changes.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eonPositionChangeEnd\u003c/code\u003e — When the position of the floating panel changes ends.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\" metastring=\"{2-5}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(floatingPanel.machine, {\n  onPositionChange(details) {\n =\u003e { position: { x: number, y: number } }\n    console.log(\"floating panel is:\", details.position.x, details.position.y)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eResize\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen the size of the floating panel changes, these callbacks are details.size.width, details.size.height)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eMinimizing and Maximizing\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe floating panel can be minimized, default, and maximized by clicking the\nrespective buttons in the header. We refer to this as the panel's \u003ccode\u003estage\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen the panel is minimized, the body is hidden and the panel is resized to a\nminimum size.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen the panel is maximized, the panel scales to the match the size of the\ndefined boundary rect (via \u003ccode\u003egetBoundaryEl\u003c/code\u003e prop).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen the panel is restored, the panel is resized back to the previously known\nsize.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen the stage changes, the \u003ccode\u003eonStageChange\u003c/code\u003e callback is
